# Test Report

Time: 2024-03-30 01:09:01.224202

### Base Program

```py
def reverse_bits(n: int) -> int:
    res = 0
    for _ in range(32):
        res <<= 1
        res |= n & 1
        n >>= 1
    return res
```

### Input

```json
[41]
```

## Test Case 1

### Modified Program

```py
def reverse_bits(n: int) -> int:
    res = 0
    for _ in range(32):
        res <<= 1
        res |= n & 1
        n >>= 1
    return res
```

<details>
<summary>parser endpoint: passed ✅</summary>

Message: 
```
Success
```

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py
def reverse_bits(var_0: int) -> int:
    res = 0
    for _ in range(32):
        res <<= 1
        res |= var_0 & 1
        var_0 >>= 1
    return res
```

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py
def reverse_bits(var_1: int) -> int:
    res = 0
    for _ in range(32):
        res <<= 1
        res |= var_1 & 1
        var_1 >>= 1
    return res
```
